int(m)\n    except:\n        return 0\n\nmaint_df['completed_minutes'] = maint_df['completed_time'].apply(time_to_minutes)\n# Sort by machine, day, completed_minutes\nmaint_df = batch_with_start['start_time'].apply(time_to_minutes)\n\nprint(f\"\\nBatch with start times: {len(batch_with_start)}\")\nprint(batch_with_start.head())\n\n# Get rejected batches from quality rejected batches with production info\nrejected_batches = rejected.merge(\n    batch_with_start[['batch_id', 'production_day', 'machine_id', 'product_id', 'start_minutes']],\n    on=['batch_id', 'product_id'],\n    how='inner'\n)\nprint(f\"Rejected batches with production info: {len(rejected_batches)}\")\nprint(rejected_batches.head())\n\n# For each rejected batch, find which maintenance no subsequent maintenance event on same machine before batch production\n\ndef find_responsible_maintenance(batch_row, maint_df):\n    \"\"\"Find the last maintenance event before this batch on the same machine.\"\"\"\n    machine = batch_row['machine_id']\n    b_day = batch_row['production_day']\n    b_min = batch_row['start_minutes']\n\n    # Filter maintenance for same machine\n    m = maint_df[maint_df['machine_id'] == machine].copy()\n    if m.empty:\n        return None\n\n    # Find events before this batch\n    # Event is before batch if: day < b_day, or (day == b_day and completed_minutes <= b_min)\n    before = m[\n        (m['day'] < b_day) |\n        ((m['day'] == b_day) & (m['completed_minutes'] <= b_min))\n    ]\n\n    if before.empty:\n        return None\n\n    # The most recent one\n    last = before.iloc[-1]  # already sorted by day, completed_minutes\n    return last\n\n# Apply to all rejected batches\nresults = []\nfor _, row in 'work_order_id': maint['work_order_id'],\n            'technician_id': maint['technician_id'],\n            'maint_day': maint['day'],\n        })\n\nresult_df = (tech_stats['n_batches'] >= 3) & (tech_stats['n_work_orders'] >= 2)\n]['technician_id'].tolist()\n\nprint(f\"\\nConfirmed technicians: {confirmed_techs}\")\n\n# For confirmed technicians, find affected products\nanswer = {}\nfor tech in confirmed_techs:\n    tech_batches = result_df[result_df['technician_id'] == tech]\n    products = sorted(tech_batches['product_id'].unique().tolist())\n    for p in products:\n        if p not in answer:\n            answer[p] = []\n        if tech not in answer[p]:\n            answer[p].append(tech)\n\n# Sort\nanswer_sorted = {}\nfor p in row['n_rejected']\n        curr_total = row['n_batches']\n\n        if curr_rejected == 0:\n            continue  # no rejections in this window, skip\n\n        if prev_total == 0:\n            # First window for this machine+product - use overall baseline\n            # Since we know overall baseline is ~0 from clean windows, any rejection is anomalous\n            # But skip for now - focus on \"change\" events\n            # Could still be a fault introduction if this is the first window after machine first service\n            # For now, let's include these if they're highly elevated\n prev_rate = prev_rejected / prev_total\n        curr_rate = curr_rejected / curr_total\n\n        # Only flag as fault introduction if:\n        # 1. Current window has significantly MORE rejections than previous\n        # 2. The increase is meaningful (not just 1 batch going from 0% to 100%)\n\n        # Condition: current rate significantly higher than prev rate using Fisher exact test\n        # 2x2 table: [[prev_rej, prev_ok], [curr_rej, curr_ok]]\n        prev_ok = prev_total - prev_rejected\n        curr_ok = curr_total - curr_rejected\n\n        if prev_ok < 0 or curr_ok < 0:\n            continue\n\n        table = [[prev_rejected, prev_ok], [curr_rejected, curr_ok]]\n        try:\n            _, pval = fisher_exact(table, alternative='less')  # less means prev rate < curr rate\n        except:\n            pval = 1.0\n\n        fault_introductions.append({\n            'work_order_id': row['work_order_id'],\n            'machine_id': machine_id,\n            'product_id': product_id,\n cumulative_rejected = 0\n    cumulative_total = 0\n    for i in range(len(grp)):\n        row = grp.iloc[i]\n        curr_rejected = row['n_rejected']\n        curr_total = row['n_batches']\n\n baseline (we know natural rate ≈ 0)\n                pval = 1.0  # mark as unknown - handle separately\n                fault_introductions.append({\n                    'work_order_id': prev_rejected\n                curr_ok = curr_total - curr_rejected\n                table = [[prev_rejected, max(prev_ok, 0)], [curr_rejected, max(curr_ok, 0)]]\n                try:\n                    _, pval = fisher_exact(table, alternative='less')\n                except:\n                    pval = 1.0\n                fault_introductions.append({\n                    'work_order_id':              'p_value': pval, 'type': 'change'\n                })\n\n        cumulative_rejected += curr_rejected\n        cumulative_total += curr_total\n\nfi_df =
